By wielding such a virtual brush, you can make vastly different marks which normally require switching between many 'brushes' in other programs. By eliminating explicit switching you can finally make expressive marks that capture your rhythm.\r\n\r\nWater-based media have always been a challenge in digital painting technology. The use of GPU makes such a simulation fast enough for real-time interaction, even on a tablet computer.\r\n\r\nFinally, the simulation is paired with a new rendering method that gives you both raster richness and vector-like output up to 12k resolution.
